This paper addresses reinforcement learning in hybrid discrete-continuous action spaces, common in robotics and control, where standard policy gradient methods suffer from poor gradient quality due to credit-assignment issues and differentiable simulators fail with discrete actions. The authors propose Hybrid Policy Optimization (HPO), which uses a mixed gradient estimator combining pathwise and score-function gradients to backpropagate through smooth parts of the simulator while maintaining unbiasedness, and reformulates action discontinuities into hybrid forms. Empirically, HPO significantly outperforms PPO on inventory control and switched linear-quadratic regulator problems, with larger gains as continuous action dimensions increase, and the cross term in the mixed gradient becomes negligible near a discrete best response, enabling variance reduction.
本文针对机器人、控制等领域常见的混合离散-连续动作空间中的强化学习问题，指出标准策略梯度方法因信用分配问题导致梯度质量差，而可微分模拟器在处理离散动作时会产生有偏梯度。作者提出混合策略优化（HPO），通过结合路径梯度和得分函数的混合梯度估计器，在平滑部分反向传播并保持无偏性，同时将动作不连续问题重构为混合形式。实验表明，HPO在库存控制和切换线性二次调节器问题上显著优于PPO，且随着连续动作维度增加性能差距扩大；混合梯度的交叉项在离散最优响应附近可忽略，从而降低方差并支持近似解耦更新。
PhyMotion: Structured 3D Motion Reward for Physics-Grounded Human Video Generation
Authors: Yidong Huang, Zun Wang, Han Lin, Dong-Ki Kim, Shayegan Omidshafiei, Jaehong Yoon, Jaemin Cho, Yue Zhang, Mohit Bansal
First: 2026-05-14T02:12:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T02:12:13+00:00
Comments: First two authors contributed equally, website: https://phy-motion.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Generating realistic human motion is a central yet unsolved challenge in video generation. While reinforcement learning (RL)-based post-training has driven recent gains in general video quality, extending it to human motion remains bottlenecked by a reward signal that cannot reliably score motion realism. Existing video rewards primarily rely on 2D perceptual signals, without explicitly modeling the 3D body state, contact, and dynamics underlying articulated human motion, and often assign high scores to videos with floating bodies or physically implausible movements. To address this, we propose PhyMotion, a structured, fine-grained motion reward that grounds recovered 3D human trajectories in a physics simulator and evaluates motion quality along multiple dimensions of physical feasibility. Concretely, we recover SMPL body meshes from generated videos, retarget them onto a humanoid in the MuJoCo physics simulator, and evaluate the resulting motion along three axes: kinematic plausibility, contact and balance consistency, and dynamic feasibility. Each component provides a continuous and interpretable signal tied to a specific aspect of motion quality, allowing the reward to capture which aspects of motion are physically correct or violated. Experiments show that PhyMotion achieves stronger correlation with human judgments than existing reward formulations. These gains carry over to RL-based post-training, where optimizing PhyMotion leads to larger and more consistent improvements than optimizing existing rewards, improving motion realism across both autoregressive and bidirectional video generators under both automatic metrics and blind human evaluation (+68 Elo gain). Ablations show that the three axes provide complementary supervision signals, while the reward preserves overall video generation quality with only modest training overhead.

生成逼真的人体运动是视频生成中一个核心但尚未解决的挑战。尽管基于强化学习（RL）的后训练已推动通用视频质量取得近期进展，但将其扩展到人体运动仍受限于无法可靠评估运动真实性的奖励信号。现有视频奖励主要依赖2D感知信号，未显式建模关节人体运动背后的3D身体状态、接触与动力学，且常对漂浮身体或物理不合理运动赋予高分。为此，我们提出PhyMotion——一种结构化、细粒度的运动奖励，它将恢复的3D人体轨迹锚定在物理模拟器中，并沿多个物理可行性维度评估运动质量。具体而言，我们从生成视频中恢复SMPL人体网格，将其重定向至MuJoCo物理模拟器中的类人模型，并沿三个轴评估所得运动：运动学合理性、接触与平衡一致性、以及动态可行性。每个分量提供与运动质量特定方面相关的连续可解释信号，使奖励能捕捉运动在物理上正确或违反的方面。实验表明，PhyMotion与人类判断的相关性优于现有奖励公式。这些优势延续至基于RL的后训练：优化PhyMotion比优化现有奖励带来更大且更一致的改进，在自回归和双向视频生成器上均提升运动真实性（自动指标和盲人评估中Elo提升+68）。消融实验表明，三个轴提供互补的监督信号，而该奖励仅以适度训练开销保持整体视频生成质量。

From Ranking to Reasoning: Explainable Web API Recommendation via Semantic Reasoning
Authors: Zishuo Xu, Dezhong Yao, Yao Wan
First: 2025-11-08T03:09:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T01:51:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid growth of Web APIs has made automated Web API recommendation essential for efficient mashup development. However, existing approaches suffer from two major limitations: 1) they rely on fixed top-N recommendation strategies that cannot adapt to mashup complexity, and 2) they provide little or no explanation for recommended APIs, limiting transparency and user trust. To address these challenges, we propose WAR-R1, an explainable Web API recommendation framework that integrates semantic reasoning with adaptive, variable-cardinality recommendation. Built on a lightweight large language model (LLM), WAR-R1 generates both a set of relevant APIs and a natural-language justification for each recommendation. To support adaptive recommendation size, we introduce special start and stop tokens that allow the model to learn when to begin and terminate API generation. WAR-R1 is trained in two stages: supervised fine-tuning on an annotated mashup-API corpus, followed by reinforcement learning using Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) with low-rank adaptation to jointly optimize recommendation accuracy and reasoning quality. Experiments on the ProgrammableWeb dataset show that WAR-R1 outperforms state-of-the-art baselines by up to 10.89% in recommendation accuracy while consistently producing high-quality, semantically grounded explanations. Extensive ablation studies validate the effectiveness of reinforcement learning, special token design, and integrated reasoning.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses limitations in existing Web API recommendation methods, which rely on fixed top-N strategies and lack explainability, by proposing WAR-R1, a framework that integrates semantic reasoning with adaptive, variable-cardinality recommendation. Built on a lightweight large language model, WAR-R1 generates both relevant APIs and natural-language justifications, using special start and stop tokens to learn adaptive recommendation sizes. The model is trained via supervised fine-tuning followed by reinforcement learning with Group Relative Policy Optimization and low-rank adaptation. Experiments on the ProgrammableWeb dataset show WAR-R1 outperforms state-of-the-art baselines by up to 10.89% in recommendation accuracy while producing high-quality, semantically grounded explanations, with ablation studies validating the contributions of reinforcement learning, special tokens, and integrated reasoning.
该论文针对现有Web API推荐方法依赖固定top-N策略且缺乏可解释性的局限，提出了WAR-R1框架，通过集成语义推理实现自适应、可变基数的推荐。该框架基于轻量级大语言模型，生成相关API集合及自然语言解释，并利用特殊起始和终止标记学习自适应推荐规模。模型训练分为两个阶段：监督微调后结合低秩适配的组相对策略优化强化学习。在ProgrammableWeb数据集上的实验表明，WAR-R1在推荐准确率上比最先进基线方法提升高达10.89%，同时持续生成高质量、有语义依据的解释，消融研究验证了强化学习、特殊标记设计和集成推理的有效性。
Towards Real-Time Autonomous Navigation: Transformer-Based Catheter Tip Tracking in Fluoroscopy
Authors: Harry Robertshaw, Yanghe Hao, Weiyuan Deng, Benjamin Jackson, S. M. Hadi Sadati, Nikola Fischer, Tom Vercauteren, Alejandro Granados, Thomas C. Booth
Venue: Int J CARS (2026)
First: 2026-05-14T01:42:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T01:42:56+00:00
Comments: Harry Robertshaw and Yanghe Hao contributed equally to this work. Published in the International Journal of Computer Assisted Radiology and Surgery
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Purpose: Mechanical thrombectomy (MT) improves stroke outcomes, but is limited by a lack of local treatment access. Widespread distribution of reinforcement learning (RL)-based robotic systems can be used to alleviate this challenge through autonomous navigation, but current RL methods require live device tip coordinate tracking to function. This paper aims to develop and evaluate a real-time catheter tip tracking pipeline under fluoroscopy, addressing challenges such as low contrast, noise, and device occlusion. Methods: A multi-threaded pipeline was designed, incorporating frame reading, preprocessing, inference, and post-processing. Deep learning segmentation models, including U-Net, U-Net+Transformer, and SegFormer, were trained and benchmarked using two-class and three-class formulations. Post-processing involved two-step component filtering, one-pixel medial skeletonization, and greedy arc-length path following with contour fall-back. Results: On manually-labeled moderate complexity fluoroscopic video data, the two-class SegFormer achieved a mean absolute error of 4.44 mm, outperforming U-Net (4.60 mm), U-Net+Transformer (6.20 mm) and all three-class models (5.19-7.74 mm). On segmentation benchmarks, the system exceeded state-of-the-art CathAction results with improvements of up to +5% in Dice scores for three-segmentation. Conclusion: The results demonstrate that the proposed multi-threaded tracking framework maintains stable performance under challenging imaging conditions, outperforming prior benchmarks, while providing a reliable and efficient foundation for RL-based autonomous MT navigation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：迈向实时自主导航：基于Transformer的透视下导管尖端追踪
目的：机械取栓（MT）可改善卒中预后，但受限于本地治疗可及性不足。通过强化学习（RL）的机器人系统广泛部署可借助自主导航缓解这一挑战，但当前RL方法需实时获取器械尖端坐标。本文旨在开发并评估透视下实时导管尖端追踪流程，应对低对比度、噪声及器械遮挡等挑战。方法：设计多线程流程，包含帧读取、预处理、推理和后处理。训练并基准测试深度学习分割模型（U-Net、U-Net+Transformer、SegFormer），采用二分类与三分类方案。后处理包括两步组件滤波、单像素中轴骨架化及带轮廓回退的贪婪弧长路径追踪。结果：在人工标注的中等复杂度透视视频数据上，二分类SegFormer平均绝对误差为4.44 mm，优于U-Net（4.60 mm）、U-Net+Transformer（6.20 mm）及所有三分类模型（5.19-7.74 mm）。在分割基准测试中，系统超越当前最优CathAction结果，三分割Dice分数提升达+5%。结论：结果表明，所提出的多线程追踪框架在挑战性成像条件下保持稳定性能，超越先前基准，为基于RL的自主MT导航提供了可靠高效的基础。

Action-Conditioned Risk Gating for Safety-Critical Control under Partial Observability
Authors: Yushen Liu, Yin-Jen Chen, Ziyi Chen, Tao Wang, Heng Huang, Xugui Zhou, Yanfu Zhang
First: 2026-05-14T01:23:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T01:23:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many safety-critical control problems are modeled as risk-sensitive partially observable Markov decision processes, where the controller must make decisions from incomplete observations while balancing task performance against safety risk. Although belief-space planning provides a principled solution, maintaining and planning over beliefs can be computationally costly and sensitive to model specification in practical domains. We propose a lightweight risk-gated reinforcement learning approximation for risk-sensitive control under partial observability. The method constructs a compact finite-history proxy state and learns an action-conditioned predictor of near-term safety violation. This predicted candidate-action risk is used in two complementary ways: as a risk penalty during value learning, and as a decision-time gate that interpolates between optimistic and conservative ensemble value estimates. As a result, low-risk actions are evaluated closer to reward-seeking estimates, while high-risk actions are evaluated more conservatively. We evaluate the approach in two safety-critical partially observable domains: automated glucose regulation and safety-constrained navigation. Across adult and adolescent glucose-control cohorts, the method improves overall glycemic tradeoffs and substantially reduces runtime relative to a belief-space planning baseline. On Safety-Gym navigation benchmarks, it achieves a more favorable reward-cost balance than unconstrained RL and several standard safe-RL baselines. These results suggest that action-conditioned near-term risk can provide an effective local signal for approximate risk-sensitive POMDP control when full belief-space planning is impractical.
Quantum Advantage in Multi Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Simranjeet Singh Dahia, Claudia Szabo
First: 2026-05-14T01:03:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T01:03:41+00:00
Comments: 19 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present an empirical evaluation of quantum entanglement in agent coordination within quantum multi agent reinforcement learning (QMARL). While QMARL has attracted growing interest recently, most prior work evaluates quantum policies without provable baselines, making it impossible to rigorously distinguish quantum advantage from algorithmic coincidence. We address this directly by evaluating a decentralized QMARL framework with variational quantum circuit (VQC) actors with shared entangled states. In the CHSH game, which has a mathematically proven classical performance ceiling of 0.75 win rate, we show that entangled QMARL agents approach the Tsirelson limit of 0.854, providing clear evidence of their quantum advantage. We show that unentangled quantum circuits match the classical baseline, confirming that entanglement and not the quantum circuit itself is the active coordination mechanism. We also explore the effect of specific entanglement structures, as some Bell states enable coordination gains while others actively harm performance. On cooperative navigation (CoopNav), QMARL without entanglement achieves $\sim2\times$ improvement in success rate over classical MAA2C ($\sim$0.85 versus $\sim$0.40), with the hybrid configuration, quantum actor paired with a classical centralised critic, outperforming both fully classical and fully quantum solutions. We present our experimental analysis and discuss future work.
中文标题/摘要
标题：量子优势在多智能体强化学习中的应用
我们提出了对量子多智能体强化学习（QMARL）中智能体协调时量子纠缠的实证评估。尽管QMARL近期吸引了越来越多的关注，但大多数先前工作在没有可证明基线的情况下评估量子策略，使得无法严格区分量子优势与算法巧合。我们通过评估一个具有共享纠缠态的变分量子电路（VQC）执行器的去中心化QMARL框架直接解决了这一问题。在CHSH博弈中，其经典性能上限在数学上被证明为0.75胜率，我们展示了纠缠QMARL智能体接近0.854的Tsirelson极限，为其量子优势提供了明确证据。我们证明非纠缠量子电路匹配经典基线，确认纠缠而非量子电路本身是活跃的协调机制。我们还探讨了特定纠缠结构的影响，因为某些贝尔态能实现协调增益，而其他则主动损害性能。在协作导航（CoopNav）中，无纠缠的QMARL在成功率上比经典MAA2C实现了约2倍的提升（约0.85对比约0.40），其中混合配置（量子执行器与经典集中式评论家配对）优于完全经典和完全量子的解决方案。我们呈现了实验分析并讨论了未来工作。

Diagnosing Training Inference Mismatch in LLM Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Tianle Zhong, Neiwen Ling, Yifan Pi, Zijun Wei, Tianshu Yu, Geoffrey Fox, Peng Wu, Xiao Yu
First: 2026-05-14T00:27:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T00:27:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern LLM RL systems separate rollout generation from policy optimization. These two stages are expected to produce token probabilities that match exactly. However, implementation differences can make them assign different values to the same sequence under the same model weights, inducing Training-Inference Mismatch (TIM). TIM is difficult to inspect because it is entangled with off-policy drift and common stabilization mechanisms. In this work, we isolate TIM in a zero-mismatch diagnostic setting (VeXact), and show that small token-level numerical disagreements can independently cause training collapse. We further show that TIM changes the effective optimization problem, and identify a set of remedies that could mitigate TIM. Our results suggest that TIM is not benign numerical noise, but a systems-level perturbation that should be treated as a first-order factor in analyzing LLM RL stability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：诊断大语言模型强化学习中的训练-推理不匹配问题
现代大语言模型强化学习系统将轨迹生成与策略优化分离。这两个阶段预期产生的词元概率应完全一致，但实现差异可能导致相同模型权重下对同一序列赋予不同数值，从而引发训练-推理不匹配（TIM）。由于TIM与离策略漂移及常见稳定机制相互纠缠，难以直接检测。本研究在零不匹配诊断环境（VeXact）中分离出TIM，证明微小的词元级数值分歧可独立导致训练崩溃。进一步揭示TIM会改变有效优化问题，并识别出一组可缓解TIM的补救措施。结果表明TIM并非良性数值噪声，而是应作为分析大语言模型强化学习稳定性的一阶因素的系统级扰动。

PreFT: Prefill-only finetuning for efficient inference
Authors: Andrew Lanpouthakoun, Aryaman Arora, Zhengxuan Wu, Dhruv Pai, Ben Keigwin, Dan Jurafsky, Christopher Potts
First: 2026-05-14T00:19:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T00:19:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models can now be personalised efficiently at scale using parameter efficient finetuning methods (PEFTs), but serving user-specific PEFTs harms throughput, even with specialised kernels and memory management techniques. This is because, theoretically and empirically, a mismatch exists between prefill (processing a large number of tokens at once) and decode (generating a single token autoregressively): the latter has far lower throughput when serving multiple adapters. Rather than optimising performance relative to parameter count, for efficient multi-adapter serving, we instead ought to optimise performance relative to serving throughput. We therefore propose PreFT (Prefill-only Finetuning), wherein we only apply the adapter to prefill tokens and discard it afterwards. PreFT significantly increases throughput with minimal effect on performance. We develop and release an efficient implementation of two prefill-only PEFTs, LoRA and ReFT, on the vLLM inference engine. We first show that serving multi-user PreFTs is more efficient than traditional PEFTs ($1.9\times$ the throughput when serving $512$ adapters on Llama 3.1 70B). Then, we compare the performance of prefill-only vs. all-token adapters on a variety of supervised finetuning and reinforcement learning tasks with LMs at varying scales. On SFT, we observe that the evaluation loss of PreFTs is higher than PEFTs, but can be compensated by increasing rank with nearly no reduction in throughput. On RL, we consistently find that PreFTs approach parity with standard PEFTs. Together, this work validates prefill-only adaptation of LLMs as a more favourable accuracy-throughput tradeoff than existing PEFTs for personalised serving.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PreFT：仅预填充微调实现高效推理
大型语言模型现可通过参数高效微调方法（PEFTs）实现规模化个性化部署，但服务用户专属PEFTs会损害吞吐量——即便采用专用内核与内存管理技术。这是因为理论与实证均表明，预填充（一次性处理大量令牌）与解码（自回归生成单个令牌）之间存在不匹配：服务多适配器时，后者的吞吐量远低于前者。为高效服务多适配器，我们不应针对参数量优化性能，而应针对服务吞吐量进行优化。为此提出PreFT（仅预填充微调），即仅对预填充令牌应用适配器，随后将其丢弃。PreFT在性能影响极小的情况下显著提升吞吐量。我们在vLLM推理引擎上开发并发布了两种仅预填充PEFT（LoRA与ReFT）的高效实现。首先证明服务多用户PreFT比传统PEFT更高效（在Llama 3.1 70B上服务512个适配器时吞吐量提升1.9倍）。随后在多种规模的语言模型上，通过监督微调与强化学习任务对比仅预填充适配器与全令牌适配器的性能。在SFT中，PreFT的评估损失高于PEFT，但可通过增加秩（几乎不降低吞吐量）进行补偿。在RL中，PreFT始终接近标准PEFT的性能。本研究验证了仅预填充适配LLM在个性化服务中相比现有PEFT具有更优的精度-吞吐量权衡。

The method applies adapters only to prefill tokens and discards them during generation, optimizing for serving throughput rather than parameter count. Experiments show that PreFT achieves 1.9x throughput improvement over standard PEFTs when serving 512 adapters on Llama 3.1 70B, and while evaluation loss on supervised finetuning tasks is slightly higher, it can be compensated by increasing rank with minimal throughput impact, and on reinforcement learning tasks, PreFT approaches parity with standard PEFTs, validating a more favorable accuracy-throughput tradeoff.
该论文提出PreFT（仅预填充微调）方法，旨在解决服务多个个性化大语言模型适配器时的吞吐量瓶颈问题，传统参数高效微调方法在解码阶段吞吐量较低。该方法仅在预填充阶段应用适配器，在生成阶段丢弃，以服务吞吐量而非参数数量为优化目标。实验表明，在Llama 3.1 70B上服务512个适配器时，PreFT的吞吐量比标准PEFT方法提升1.9倍；在监督微调任务中，虽然评估损失略高，但可通过增加秩来补偿且几乎不影响吞吐量，在强化学习任务中，PreFT接近标准PEFT的性能，验证了其在准确率与吞吐量之间更优的权衡。
GenCircuit-RL: Reinforcement Learning from Hierarchical Verification for Genetic Circuit Design
Authors: Noah Flynn
Venue: icml poster
First: 2026-05-14T00:18:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T00:18:09+00:00
Comments: Link: https://icml.cc/virtual/2026/poster/61789
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Genetic circuit design remains a laborious, expert-driven process despite decades of progress in synthetic biology. We study this problem through code generation: models produce Python code in pysbol3 to construct genetic circuits in the Synthetic Biology Open Language (SBOL), a formal representation that supports automated verification. We introduce GenCircuit-RL, a reinforcement learning framework built around hierarchical verification rewards that decompose correctness into five levels, from code execution to task-specific topological checks, and a four-stage curriculum that shifts optimization pressure from code generation to functional reasoning. We also introduce SynBio-Reason, a benchmark of 4,753 circuits spanning six canonical circuit types and nine tasks from code repair to de novo design, with held-out biological parts for out-of-distribution evaluation. Hierarchical verification improves task success on functional reasoning tasks by 14 to 16 percentage points over binary rewards, and curriculum learning is required for strong design performance. The resulting models generate topologically correct circuits, generalize to novel biological parts, and rediscover canonical designs from the synthetic biology literature.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GenCircuit-RL：基于分层验证的强化学习用于基因电路设计
尽管合成生物学已取得数十年进展，基因电路设计仍是一个劳动密集且依赖专家经验的过程。我们通过代码生成研究该问题：模型生成pysbol3格式的Python代码，以构建合成生物学开放语言（SBOL）中的基因电路——这是一种支持自动验证的形式化表示。我们提出GenCircuit-RL，一种围绕分层验证奖励构建的强化学习框架，将正确性分解为从代码执行到任务特定拓扑检查的五个层级，并采用四阶段课程学习，将优化压力从代码生成转向功能推理。我们还引入SynBio-Reason基准，包含4,753个电路，涵盖六种标准电路类型和从代码修复到全新设计的九项任务，并采用保留的生物部件进行分布外评估。分层验证在功能推理任务上比二元奖励提升了14至16个百分点的任务成功率，而课程学习是实现强设计性能的必要条件。最终模型能生成拓扑正确的电路，泛化至新型生物部件，并重新发现合成生物学文献中的经典设计。

MetaAgent-X : Breaking the Ceiling of Automatic Multi-Agent Systems via End-to-End Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yaolun Zhang, Yujie Zhao, Nan Wang, Yiran Wu, Jiayu Chang, Yizhao Chen, Qingyun Wu, Jishen Zhao, Huazheng Wang
First: 2026-05-14T00:11:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T00:11:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Automatic multi-agent systems aim to instantiate agent workflows without relying on manually designed or fixed orchestration. However, existing automatic MAS approaches remain only partially adaptive: they either perform training-free test-time search or optimize the meta-level designer while keeping downstream execution agents frozen, which creating a frozen-executor ceiling and leaving the end-to-end training of self-designing and self-executing agentic models unexplored. To address this, we introduce MetaAgent-X, an end-to-end reinforcement learning framework that jointly optimizes automatic MAS design and execution. MetaAgent-X enables script-based MAS generation, execution rollout collection, and credit assignment for both designer and executor trajectories. To support stable and scalable optimization, we propose Executor Designer Hierarchical Rollout and Stagewise Co-evolution to improve training stability and expose the dynamics of designer-executor co-evolution. MetaAgent-X consistently outperforms existing automatic MAS baselines, achieving up to 21.7% gains. Comprehensive ablations show that both designer and executor improve throughout training, and that effective automatic MAS learning follows a stagewise co-evolution process. These results establish end-to-end trainable automatic MAS as a practical paradigm for building self-designing and self-executing agentic models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MetaAgent-X：通过端到端强化学习突破自动多智能体系统的性能上限
自动多智能体系统旨在无需人工设计或固定编排的情况下实例化智能体工作流。然而，现有的自动MAS方法仅具有部分自适应性：它们要么执行无训练的测试时搜索，要么在冻结下游执行智能体的同时优化元级设计器，这造成了“冻结执行器”的性能天花板，且尚未探索自设计与自执行智能体模型的端到端训练。为解决这一问题，我们提出MetaAgent-X，一种联合优化自动MAS设计与执行的端到端强化学习框架。MetaAgent-X支持基于脚本的MAS生成、执行轨迹收集，以及针对设计器和执行器轨迹的信用分配。为支持稳定且可扩展的优化，我们提出“执行器-设计器分层展开”与“阶段式协同进化”方法，以提升训练稳定性并揭示设计器与执行器协同进化的动态过程。MetaAgent-X持续优于现有自动MAS基线，性能提升最高达21.7%。全面的消融实验表明，设计器和执行器在训练过程中均持续改进，且有效的自动MAS学习遵循阶段式协同进化过程。这些结果确立了端到端可训练的自动MAS作为构建自设计与自执行智能体模型的实用范式。

Existing automatic multi-agent systems are only partially adaptive, as they either perform training-free test-time search or optimize only the meta-level designer while keeping execution agents frozen, creating a ceiling on performance. To address this, the authors propose MetaAgent-X, an end-to-end reinforcement learning framework that jointly optimizes both the design and execution of multi-agent systems through script-based generation, rollout collection, and credit assignment for both designer and executor trajectories. Stable and scalable optimization is achieved via Executor Designer Hierarchical Rollout and Stagewise Co-evolution. MetaAgent-X consistently outperforms existing baselines, achieving up to 21.7% gains, with ablations confirming that both designer and executor improve throughout training and that effective learning follows a stagewise co-evolution process.
现有的自动多智能体系统仅具有部分自适应性，它们要么进行无需训练的测试时搜索，要么仅优化元级设计者而冻结下游执行智能体，从而造成了性能天花板。为了解决这一问题，作者提出了MetaAgent-X，一种端到端的强化学习框架，通过基于脚本的生成、执行轨迹收集以及为设计者和执行者轨迹分配信用，联合优化自动多智能体系统的设计与执行。通过执行者-设计者分层展开和阶段性协同进化，实现了稳定且可扩展的优化。MetaAgent-X持续优于现有基线方法，性能提升最高达21.7%，消融实验证实设计者和执行者在训练过程中均得到改进，且有效的自动多智能体学习遵循阶段性协同进化过程。
AgentForesight: Online Auditing for Early Failure Prediction in Multi-Agent Systems
Authors: Boxuan Zhang, Jianing Zhu, Zeru Shi, Dongfang Liu, Ruixiang Tang
First: 2026-05-09T05:55:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T23:06:48+00:00
Comments: 33 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
LLM-based multi-agent systems are increasingly deployed on long-horizon tasks, but a single decisive error is often accepted by downstream agents and cascades into trajectory-level failure. Existing work frames this as \emph{post-hoc failure attribution}, diagnosing the responsible agent and step after the trajectory has ended. However, this paradigm forfeits any opportunity to intervene while trajectory is still unfolding. In this work, we introduce AgentForesight, a framework that reframes this problem as online auditing: at each step of an unfolding trajectory, an auditor observes only the current prefix and must either continue the run or alarm at the earliest decisive error, without access to future steps. To this end, we curate AFTraj-2K, a corpus of agentic trajectories across Coding, Math, and Agentic domains, in which safe trajectories are retained under a strict curation pipeline and unsafe trajectories are annotated at the step of their decisive error via consensus among multiple LLM judges. Built on that, we develop AgentForesight-7B, a compact online auditor trained with a coarse-to-fine reinforcement learning recipe that first equips it with a risk-anticipation prior at the failure boundary on adjacent safe/unsafe prefix pairs, then sharpens this prior into precise step-level localization under a three-axis reward jointly targeting the what, where, and who of an audit verdict. Across AFTraj-2K and an external Who\&When benchmark, AgentForesight-7B outperforms leading proprietary models, including GPT-4.1 and DeepSeek-V4-Pro, achieving up to +19.9% performance gain and 3$\times$ lower step localization error, opening the loop from post-hoc failures detection to enabling deployment-time intervention. Project page: https://zbox1005.github.io/agent-foresight/
中文标题/摘要
标题：AgentForesight：多智能体系统中早期故障预测的在线审计
基于大语言模型的多智能体系统越来越多地部署在长周期任务上，但单个决定性错误往往被下游智能体接受并级联为轨迹级故障。现有工作将此框架化为事后故障归因，在轨迹结束后诊断责任智能体和步骤。然而，这种范式放弃了在轨迹仍在展开时进行干预的任何机会。在本工作中，我们引入AgentForesight，一个将问题重新定义为在线审计的框架：在展开轨迹的每一步，审计员仅观察当前前缀，必须要么继续运行，要么在最早的决定性错误处发出警报，且无法访问未来步骤。为此，我们整理了AFTraj-2K，一个涵盖编码、数学和智能体领域的智能体轨迹语料库，其中安全轨迹在严格筛选流程下保留，不安全轨迹通过多个大语言模型评判者之间的共识在其决定性错误步骤处进行标注。在此基础上，我们开发了AgentForesight-7B，一个紧凑的在线审计员，通过从粗到细的强化学习方案训练，该方案首先在相邻安全/不安全前缀对的失败边界上赋予其风险预期先验，然后在同时针对审计判决的什么、哪里和谁的三轴奖励下，将此先验锐化为精确的步骤级定位。在AFTraj-2K和外部Who&When基准上，AgentForesight-7B优于领先的专有模型，包括GPT-4.1和DeepSeek-V4-Pro，实现了高达+19.9%的性能提升和3倍的步骤定位误差降低，从而打开了从事后故障检测到部署时干预的闭环。项目页面：https://zbox1005.github.io/agent-foresight/
Summary / 总结
AgentForesight addresses the limitation of existing post-hoc failure attribution methods in LLM-based multi-agent systems, which only diagnose errors after trajectory completion and thus miss opportunities for real-time intervention. The framework reframes failure detection as online auditing, where an auditor observes each step of an unfolding trajectory and must decide to either continue or raise an alarm at the earliest decisive error without future knowledge. To support this, the authors curate AFTraj-2K, a corpus of agentic trajectories with step-level annotations of decisive errors, and train AgentForesight-7B using a coarse-to-fine reinforcement learning approach that first establishes a risk-anticipation prior on adjacent safe/unsafe prefix pairs and then refines it into precise step-level localization via a three-axis reward. Experiments on AFTraj-2K and the external Who&When benchmark show that AgentForesight-7B outperforms leading proprietary models like GPT-4.1 and DeepSeek-V4-Pro, achieving up to +19.9% performance gain and 3× lower step localization error, enabling deployment-time intervention.
AgentForesight 针对现有基于大语言模型的多智能体系统中事后故障归因方法的局限性，这些方法仅在轨迹完成后诊断错误，从而错失了实时干预的机会。该框架将故障检测重新定义为在线审计，审计员在轨迹展开的每一步观察当前前缀，并在无法获取未来信息的情况下决定继续运行还是尽早发出警报。为此，作者构建了 AFTraj-2K 语料库，其中包含带有步骤级决定性错误标注的智能体轨迹，并通过从粗到细的强化学习训练了 AgentForesight-7B 模型：首先在相邻的安全/不安全前缀对上建立风险预期先验，然后通过三轴奖励将其优化为精确的步骤级定位。在 AFTraj-2K 和外部 Who&When 基准上的实验表明，AgentForesight-7B 优于 GPT-4.1 和 DeepSeek-V4-Pro 等领先专有模型，实现了高达 +19.9% 的性能提升和 3 倍的步骤定位误差降低，从而将事后故障检测转变为部署时的实时干预。
Knowing When to Quit: A Principled Framework for Dynamic Abstention in LLM Reasoning
Authors: Hen Davidov, Nachshon Cohen, Oren Kalinsky, Yaron Fairstein, Guy Kushilevitz, Ram Yazdi, Patrick Rebeschini
First: 2026-04-20T15:38:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T21:27:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLMs utilizing chain-of-thought reasoning often waste substantial compute by producing long, incorrect responses. Abstention can mitigate this by withholding outputs unlikely to be correct. While most abstention methods decide to withhold outputs before or after generation, dynamic mid-generation abstention considers early termination of unpromising reasoning traces at each token position. Prior work has explored empirical variants of this idea, but principled guidance for the abstention rule remains lacking. We present a formal analysis of dynamic abstention for LLMs, modeling abstention as an explicit action within a regularized reinforcement learning framework. An abstention reward parameter controls the trade-off between compute and information. We show that abstaining when the value function falls below this reward strictly outperforms natural baselines under general conditions. We further derive a principled and efficient method to approximate the value function. Empirical results on mathematical reasoning and toxicity avoidance tasks support our theory and demonstrate improved selective accuracy over existing methods.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the problem of LLMs wasting computational resources on long, incorrect chain-of-thought reasoning by proposing a principled framework for dynamic abstention during generation. The authors model abstention as an explicit action within a regularized reinforcement learning framework, introducing an abstention reward parameter to balance compute and information. They derive a rule to abstain when the value function falls below this reward, which theoretically outperforms baselines, and provide an efficient approximation method. Experiments on mathematical reasoning and toxicity avoidance tasks show improved selective accuracy over existing methods.
该论文针对大型语言模型在链式思维推理中因生成冗长错误答案而浪费计算资源的问题，提出了一种动态中途放弃的原则性框架。作者将放弃建模为带正则化的强化学习框架中的显式动作，通过引入放弃奖励参数来平衡计算与信息。他们推导出当价值函数低于该奖励时放弃的规则，理论上优于基线方法，并提供了高效的价值函数近似方法。在数学推理和毒性避免任务上的实验表明，该方法相比现有方法提升了选择性准确率。
Reinforcement Learning for Tool-Calling Agents in Fast Healthcare Interoperability Resources (FHIR)
Authors: Marius S. Knorr, Robert Müller, Jan P. Bremer, Nils Schweingruber
First: 2026-05-13T21:27:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T21:27:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Fast Healthcare Interoperability Resources (FHIR) is the dominant standard for interoperable exchange of healthcare data. In FHIR, electronic health records form a directed graph of resources. Answering clinically meaningful questions over FHIR requires agents to perform multi-step reasoning, filtering, and aggregation across multiple resource types. Prior work shows that even tool-augmented LLM agents (retrieval, code execution, multi-turn planning) often select the wrong resources or violate traversal constraints. We study this problem in the context of FHIR-AgentBench, a benchmark for realistic question answering over real-world hospital data, and frame reasoning on FHIR as a sequential decision-making problem over a queryable structured graph. We implement a multi-turn CodeAct agent and post-train it with reinforcement learning using a custom harness and tools. A LLM Judge provides execution-grounded rewards. Compared to prompt-based, closed-model baselines, RL post-training improves performance while enforcing data-integrity constraints. Empirically, our approach improves answer correctness from 50% (o4-mini) to 77% on FHIR-AgentBench using a smaller and cheaper Qwen3-8B model. We present an end-to-end post-training pipeline (environment building, harness construction, model training and custom evaluation) that reliably improves multi-turn reasoning over structured clinical graphs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向快速医疗互操作性资源（FHIR）中工具调用代理的强化学习
快速医疗互操作性资源（FHIR）是医疗数据互操作交换的主流标准。在FHIR中，电子健康记录构成一个有向资源图。回答FHIR上的临床有意义问题需要代理跨多种资源类型执行多步推理、过滤和聚合。先前研究表明，即使经过工具增强的大语言模型代理（检索、代码执行、多轮规划）也常选错资源或违反遍历约束。我们在FHIR-AgentBench（一个基于真实医院数据的现实问答基准）背景下研究此问题，并将FHIR上的推理形式化为可查询结构化图上的序列决策问题。我们实现了一个多轮CodeAct代理，并使用自定义工具集和强化学习对其进行后训练。大语言模型评判器提供基于执行结果的奖励。与基于提示的封闭模型基线相比，强化学习后训练在提升性能的同时强制执行数据完整性约束。实验表明，我们的方法使用更小更便宜的Qwen3-8B模型，将FHIR-AgentBench上的答案正确率从50%（o4-mini）提升至77%。我们提出了一个端到端的后训练流程（环境构建、工具集构建、模型训练和自定义评估），可可靠地提升结构化临床图上的多轮推理能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of answering clinically meaningful questions over Fast Healthcare Interoperability Resources (FHIR), a standard for healthcare data exchange, where electronic health records form a directed graph requiring multi-step reasoning. The authors frame this as a sequential decision-making problem and implement a multi-turn CodeAct agent post-trained with reinforcement learning, using a custom harness and an LLM Judge for execution-grounded rewards. Experimental results on the FHIR-AgentBench benchmark show that this approach improves answer correctness from 50% with o4-mini to 77% using a smaller Qwen3-8B model, while enforcing data-integrity constraints.
本文针对快速医疗互操作性资源（FHIR）标准下回答临床有意义问题的挑战，其中电子健康记录构成有向图，需要多步推理。作者将问题建模为序列决策过程，实现了一个多轮CodeAct智能体，并通过强化学习进行后训练，使用自定义框架和LLM裁判提供基于执行的奖励。在FHIR-AgentBench基准上的实验结果表明，该方法使用更小更便宜的Qwen3-8B模型，将答案正确率从o4-mini的50%提升至77%，同时保证了数据完整性约束。
LoVeC: Reinforcement Learning for Better Verbalized Confidence in Long-Form Generations
Authors: Caiqi Zhang, Xiaochen Zhu, Chengzu Li, Nigel Collier, Andreas Vlachos
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-05-29T18:05:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T21:21:09+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 Main
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Hallucination remains a major challenge for the safe and trustworthy deployment of large language models (LLMs) in factual content generation. Prior work has explored confidence estimation as an effective approach to hallucination detection, but often relies on post-hoc self-consistency methods that require computationally expensive sampling. Verbalized confidence offers a more efficient alternative, but existing approaches are largely limited to short-form question answering (QA) tasks and do not generalize well to open-ended generation. In this paper, we propose LoVeC (Long-form Verbalized Confidence), a novel reinforcement learning based method that trains LLMs to append an on-the-fly numerical confidence score to each generated statement during long-form generation. The confidence score serves as a direct and interpretable signal of the factuality of generation. We introduce two evaluation settings, free-form tagging and iterative tagging, to assess different verbalized confidence estimation methods. Experiments on three long-form QA datasets show that our RL-trained models achieve better calibration and generalize robustly across domains. Also, our method is highly efficient, being 20 times faster than traditional self-consistency methods while achieving better calibration.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LoVeC：基于强化学习的长文本生成中更优口头置信度
幻觉仍然是大型语言模型在事实性内容生成中安全可信部署的主要挑战。先前工作探索了置信度估计作为幻觉检测的有效方法，但通常依赖于需要计算昂贵采样的后验自洽性方法。口头置信度提供了一种更高效的替代方案，但现有方法主要局限于短文本问答任务，难以泛化到开放式生成。本文提出LoVeC（长文本口头置信度），一种基于强化学习的新方法，训练LLM在长文本生成过程中为每个生成的陈述附加实时数值置信度分数。该置信度分数作为生成事实性的直接可解释信号。我们引入两种评估设置——自由形式标记和迭代标记——以评估不同的口头置信度估计方法。在三个长文本问答数据集上的实验表明，我们的RL训练模型实现了更好的校准，并在不同领域稳健泛化。此外，我们的方法高效，比传统自洽性方法快20倍，同时实现更好的校准。
Summary / 总结
LoVeC addresses the challenge of hallucination in long-form text generation by proposing a reinforcement learning method that trains large language models to output a numerical confidence score for each generated statement in real time. This approach improves upon prior verbalized confidence methods that are limited to short-form QA, and it avoids the computational expense of post-hoc self-consistency techniques. Experiments on three long-form QA datasets demonstrate that the RL-trained models achieve better calibration and robust cross-domain generalization, while being 20 times faster than traditional self-consistency methods.
LoVeC针对长文本生成中的幻觉问题，提出了一种基于强化学习的方法，训练大语言模型在生成每个语句时实时输出一个数值置信度分数。该方法改进了此前仅适用于短问答的言语化置信度方法，并避免了事后自一致性技术的高计算成本。在三个长问答数据集上的实验表明，经过强化学习训练的模型实现了更好的校准和稳健的跨领域泛化，同时比传统自一致性方法快20倍。
Generative Floor Plan Design with LLMs via Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards
Authors: Luis Lara, Aristides Milios, Zhi Hao Luo, Aditya Sharma, Ge Ya Luo, Christopher Beckham, Florian Golemo, Christopher Pal
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-05-13T21:06:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T21:06:12+00:00
Comments: Accepted to Findings of ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
An AI system for professional floor plan design must precisely control room dimensions and areas while respecting the desired connectivity between rooms and maintaining functional and aesthetic quality. Existing generative approaches focus primarily on respecting the requested connectivity between rooms, but do not support generating floor plans that respect numerical constraints. We introduce a text-based floor plan generation approach that fine-tunes a large language model (LLM) on real plans and then applies reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) to improve adherence to topological and numerical constraints while discouraging invalid or overlapping outputs. Furthermore, we design a set of constraint adherence metrics to systematically measure how generated floor plans align with user-defined constraints. Our model generates floor plans that satisfy user-defined connectivity and numerical constraints and outperforms existing methods on Realism, Compatibility, and Diversity metrics. Across all tasks, our approach achieves at least a 94% relative reduction in Compatibility compared with existing methods. Our results demonstrate that LLMs can effectively handle constraints in this setting, suggesting broader applications for text-based generative modeling.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于强化学习与可验证奖励的LLM生成式户型设计
专业户型设计的AI系统需精确控制房间尺寸与面积，同时兼顾房间间连通性要求及功能美学质量。现有生成方法主要关注连通性约束，但无法支持满足数值约束的户型生成。我们提出一种基于文本的户型生成方法：先在大规模真实户型数据上微调大语言模型，再应用带可验证奖励的强化学习提升拓扑与数值约束的遵循度，同时抑制无效或重叠输出。此外，我们设计了一套约束遵循度指标，系统衡量生成户型与用户定义约束的匹配程度。该模型生成的户型能同时满足连通性与数值约束，在真实性、兼容性和多样性指标上均优于现有方法。在所有任务中，我们的方法相比现有方法在兼容性上实现了至少94%的相对降低。结果表明，大语言模型能有效处理此类约束，为基于文本的生成建模提供了更广阔的应用前景。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of generating professional floor plans that must satisfy both topological connectivity and precise numerical constraints on room dimensions and areas. The authors propose a text-based approach that fine-tunes a large language model on real floor plans and then applies reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards to improve adherence to these constraints while penalizing invalid or overlapping outputs. They also design systematic metrics to measure constraint adherence. Experimental results show that their method outperforms existing approaches on Realism, Compatibility, and Diversity, achieving at least a 94% relative reduction in Compatibility error, demonstrating that LLMs can effectively handle constrained generation tasks.
该论文针对专业户型图生成中需同时满足房间拓扑连接和精确尺寸数值约束的挑战，提出了一种基于文本的生成方法。该方法先在大规模真实户型图上微调大语言模型，再通过带可验证奖励的强化学习来提升模型对拓扑和数值约束的遵守程度，同时抑制无效或重叠输出。作者还设计了一套约束遵守度量指标。实验结果表明，该方法在真实性、兼容性和多样性指标上均优于现有方法，兼容性误差相对降低至少94%，证明了大语言模型能有效处理此类约束生成任务。
DUET: Optimizing Training Data Mixtures via Feedback from Unseen Evaluation Tasks
Authors: Zhiliang Chen, Gregory Kang Ruey Lau, Chuan-Sheng Foo, Bryan Kian Hsiang Low
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-02-01T01:52:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T20:43:28+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026 main conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The performance of an LLM depends heavily on the relevance of its training data to the downstream evaluation task. However, in practice, the data involved in an unseen evaluation task is often unknown (e.g., conversations between an LLM and a user are end-to-end encrypted). Hence, it is unclear what data are relevant for fine-tuning the LLM to maximize its performance on the specific unseen evaluation task. Instead, one can only deploy the LLM on the unseen task to gather multiple rounds of feedback on how well the model performs (e.g., user ratings). This novel setting offers a refreshing perspective towards optimizing training data mixtures via feedback from an unseen evaluation task, which prior data mixing and selection works do not consider. Our paper presents DUET, a novel global-to-local algorithm that interleaves influence function as a data selection method with Bayesian optimization to optimize data mixture via feedback from a specific unseen evaluation task. By analyzing DUET's cumulative regret, we theoretically show that DUET converges to the optimal training data mixture for an unseen task even without any data knowledge of the task. Finally, our experiments across a variety of language tasks demonstrate that DUET outperforms existing data selection and mixing methods in the unseen-task setting.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DUET：通过未见评估任务的反馈优化训练数据混合
大型语言模型的性能在很大程度上取决于其训练数据与下游评估任务的相关性。然而，在实践中，未见评估任务所涉及的数据通常是未知的（例如，LLM与用户之间的对话是端到端加密的）。因此，不清楚哪些数据与微调LLM以最大化其在特定未见评估任务上的性能相关。相反，只能将LLM部署在未见任务上，以收集多轮关于模型表现如何的反馈（例如，用户评分）。这种新颖的设置提供了一种通过未见评估任务的反馈来优化训练数据混合的全新视角，这是先前的数据混合和选择工作未曾考虑的。我们的论文提出了DUET，一种新颖的全局到局部算法，它将影响函数作为数据选择方法与贝叶斯优化交织在一起，通过特定未见评估任务的反馈来优化数据混合。通过分析DUET的累积遗憾，我们从理论上证明，即使对该任务没有任何数据知识，DUET也能收敛到未见任务的最优训练数据混合。最后，我们在各种语言任务上的实验表明，在未见任务设置中，DUET优于现有的数据选择和混合方法。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of optimizing training data mixtures for large language models when the evaluation task is unseen and its data is unknown, such as in encrypted user interactions. The authors propose DUET, a global-to-local algorithm that combines influence functions for data selection with Bayesian optimization to iteratively refine the data mixture based solely on feedback from the unseen task. Theoretical analysis shows DUET converges to the optimal mixture with bounded cumulative regret, and experiments across various language tasks demonstrate that it outperforms existing data selection and mixing methods in this novel setting.
该论文针对大语言模型在评估任务未知且其数据不可见（如加密的用户交互）时，如何优化训练数据混合的问题。作者提出DUET算法，这是一种全局到局部的算法，它将影响函数作为数据选择方法与贝叶斯优化相结合，仅基于未知任务的反馈迭代优化数据混合。理论分析表明DUET的累积遗憾有界，能收敛到最优数据混合，且在多种语言任务上的实验证明，它在此新设定下优于现有数据选择与混合方法。
Bad Seeing or Bad Thinking? Rewarding Perception for Vision-Language Reasoning
Authors: Haozhe Wang, Qixin Xu, Changpeng Wang, Taofeng Xue, Chong Peng, Wenhu Chen, Fangzhen Lin
Venue: ICML 2026 Spotlight
First: 2026-05-13T19:23:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T19:23:53+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICML 2026 as Spotlight
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Achieving robust perception-reasoning synergy is a central goal for advanced Vision-Language Models (VLMs). Recent advancements have pursued this goal via architectural designs or agentic workflows. However, these approaches are often limited by static textual reasoning or complicated by the significant compute and engineering burden of external agentic complexity. Worse, this heavy investment does not yield proportional gains, often witnessing a "seesaw effect" on perception and reasoning. This motivates a fundamental rethinking of the true bottleneck. In this paper, we argue that the root cause of this trade-off is an ambiguity in modality credit assignment: when a VLM fails, is it due to flawed perception ("bad seeing") or flawed logic ("bad thinking")? To resolve this, we introduce a reinforcement learning framework that improves perception-reasoning synergy by reliably rewarding the perception fidelity. We explicitly decompose the generation process into interleaved perception and reasoning steps. This decoupling enables targeted supervision on perception. Crucially, we introduce Perception Verification (PV), leveraging a "blindfolded reasoning" proxy to reward perceptual fidelity independently of reasoning outcomes. Furthermore, to scale training across free-form VL tasks, we propose Structured Verbal Verification, which replaces high-variance LLM judging with structured algorithmic execution. These techniques are integrated into a Modality-Aware Credit Assignment (MoCA) mechanism, which routes rewards to the specific source of error -- either bad seeing or bad thinking -- enabling a single VLM to achieve simultaneous performance gains across a wide task spectrum.
中文标题/摘要
标题：视觉不佳还是思维有误？为视觉-语言推理奖励感知能力
实现稳健的感知-推理协同是高级视觉-语言模型（VLM）的核心目标。近期进展通过架构设计或智能体工作流追求这一目标，但这些方法常受限于静态文本推理，或因外部智能体复杂性带来的巨大计算与工程负担而变得复杂。更糟的是，这种高投入并未带来相应收益，反而常出现感知与推理间的“跷跷板效应”。这促使我们从根本上重新思考真正的瓶颈。本文认为，这种权衡的根本原因是模态信用分配中的歧义：当VLM失败时，是由于感知缺陷（“视觉不佳”）还是逻辑缺陷（“思维有误”）？为解决此问题，我们引入一种强化学习框架，通过可靠奖励感知保真度来提升感知-推理协同。我们明确将生成过程分解为交错的感知与推理步骤，这种解耦使得对感知的定向监督成为可能。关键地，我们提出感知验证（PV），利用“盲推理”代理独立于推理结果奖励感知保真度。此外，为将训练扩展到自由形式VL任务，我们提出结构化口头验证，用结构化算法执行替代高方差LLM评判。这些技术被整合到模态感知信用分配（MoCA）机制中，该机制将奖励路由到特定错误源——无论是视觉不佳还是思维有误——使单个VLM能在广泛任务谱上同时获得性能提升。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the trade-off between perception and reasoning in Vision-Language Models (VLMs), which the authors attribute to ambiguity in modality credit assignment—whether a failure stems from flawed perception ('bad seeing') or flawed logic ('bad thinking'). To resolve this, they propose a reinforcement learning framework that improves perception-reasoning synergy by explicitly decomposing the generation process into interleaved perception and reasoning steps, enabling targeted supervision on perception. They introduce Perception Verification (PV), which uses a 'blindfolded reasoning' proxy to reward perceptual fidelity independently of reasoning outcomes, and Structured Verbal Verification to scale training across free-form tasks. Integrated into a Modality-Aware Credit Assignment (MoCA) mechanism, this approach routes rewards to the specific error source, achieving simultaneous performance gains across a wide task spectrum, as demonstrated in their experiments.
本文针对视觉语言模型（VLM）中感知与推理之间的权衡问题，将其归因于模态信用分配的模糊性——即失败源于感知缺陷（'看不好'）还是逻辑缺陷（'想不好'）。为解决此问题，他们提出一种强化学习框架，通过将生成过程显式分解为交错的感知与推理步骤，实现对感知的定向监督，从而提升感知-推理协同性。该框架引入感知验证（PV），利用'盲推理'代理独立于推理结果奖励感知保真度，并采用结构化口头验证以在自由形式任务上扩展训练。这些技术集成于模态感知信用分配（MoCA）机制中，将奖励路由至具体的错误来源，实验表明该方法能在广泛任务上同时提升性能。
R2R2: Robust Representation for Intensive Experience Reuse via Redundancy Reduction in Self-Predictive Learning
Authors: Sanghyeob Song, Donghyeok Lee, Jinsik Kim, Sungroh Yoon
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-05-13T18:38:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T18:38:32+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the Forty-Third International Conference on Machine Learning (ICML 2026). This is the camera-ready version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
For reinforcement learning in data-scarce domains like real-world robotics, intensive data reuse enhances efficiency but induces overfitting. While prior works focus on critic bias, representation-level instability in Self-Predictive Learning (SPL) under high Update-to-Data (UTD) regimes remains underexplored. To bridge this gap, we propose Robust Representation via Redundancy Reduction (R2R2), a regularization method within SPL. We theoretically identify that standard zero-centering conflicts with SPL's spectral properties and design a non-centered objective accordingly. We verify R2R2 on SPL-native algorithms like TD7. Furthermore, to demonstrate its orthogonality to prior advancements, we extend the state-of-the-art SimbaV2, which originally lacks SPL, by integrating a tailored SPL module, termed SimbaV2-SPL. Experiments across 11 continuous control tasks confirm that R2R2 effectively mitigates overfitting; specifically, at a UTD ratio of 20, it improves TD7 by ~22% and provides additional gains on top of SimbaV2-SPL, which itself establishes a new state-of-the-art. The code can be found at: https://github.com/songsang7/R2R2
中文标题/摘要
标题：R2R2：通过自预测学习中的冗余减少实现密集经验复用的鲁棒表示
在数据稀缺领域（如真实世界机器人）的强化学习中，密集数据复用可提升效率但易导致过拟合。现有工作主要关注评论家偏差，而高更新-数据比（UTD）下自预测学习（SPL）中表示层面的不稳定性仍未被充分探索。为弥补这一空白，我们提出鲁棒表示通过冗余减少（R2R2），一种在SPL框架内的正则化方法。我们从理论上证明标准零中心化与SPL的谱特性存在冲突，并据此设计了一个非中心化目标。我们在TD7等SPL原生算法上验证了R2R2。此外，为展示其与先前进展的正交性，我们通过集成定制SPL模块扩展了原本缺乏SPL的最先进方法SimbaV2，称为SimbaV2-SPL。在11个连续控制任务上的实验证实，R2R2有效缓解过拟合；具体而言，在UTD比为20时，它使TD7提升约22%，并在SimbaV2-SPL（其本身已建立新最先进水平）基础上带来额外增益。代码见：https://github.com/songsang7/R2R2
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses overfitting in reinforcement learning under high update-to-data (UTD) regimes, particularly focusing on representation-level instability in Self-Predictive Learning (SPL). The authors propose Robust Representation via Redundancy Reduction (R2R2), a regularization method that resolves a theoretical conflict between standard zero-centering and SPL's spectral properties by introducing a non-centered objective. Experiments on 11 continuous control tasks show that R2R2 improves TD7 by approximately 22% at a UTD ratio of 20 and provides additional gains when integrated into the state-of-the-art SimbaV2-SPL framework, establishing a new benchmark.
本文针对强化学习在高更新-数据比（UTD）下的过拟合问题，聚焦于自预测学习（SPL）中未被充分探索的表征级不稳定性。作者提出鲁棒表征冗余减少（R2R2）正则化方法，通过设计非中心化目标，从理论上解决了标准零中心化与SPL谱特性之间的冲突。在11个连续控制任务上的实验表明，R2R2在UTD比为20时使TD7提升约22%，并在集成到最新SimbaV2-SPL框架后带来额外增益，确立了新的性能基准。
Training and Evaluating Language Models with Template-based Data Generation
Authors: Yifan Zhang
Venue: ICLR 2025
First: 2024-11-27T07:32:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T18:33:16+00:00
Comments: Published in ICLR 2025 DATA-FM Workshop. Project Page: https://github.com/iiis-ai/TemplateMath
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The rapid advancement of large language models (LLMs) such as GPT-3, PaLM, and Llama has significantly transformed natural language processing, showcasing remarkable capabilities in understanding and generating language. However, a fundamental bottleneck persists: these models often struggle with tasks requiring complex, multi-step reasoning, particularly in mathematical problem-solving. This deficiency stems from the critical scarcity of large-scale, high-quality, domain-specific datasets necessary for cultivating sophisticated reasoning abilities. To overcome this challenge, we introduce Template-based Data Generation (TDG), a novel and scalable paradigm that harnesses frontier LLMs (GPT-4) to automatically generate parameterized meta-templates, which in turn synthesize a virtually infinite stream of high-quality problems and solutions. Using this paradigm, we create TemplateMath Part I: TemplateGSM, a foundational dataset of over 7 million synthetically generated grade school math problems. Each problem is accompanied by a programmatically verifiable solution, offering an unprecedented level of quality at scale. This resource not only resolves the data scarcity issue for supervised fine-tuning but also provides a robust mechanism for model alignment through Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR). Our approach elevates data augmentation by leveraging GPT-4 to generate meta-templates, ensuring diverse and complex problem structures. By providing a scalable solution to the data and verification bottleneck, TDG and TemplateGSM pave the way for a new generation of LLMs with powerful, reliable reasoning skills.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于模板数据生成的语言模型训练与评估
GPT-3、PaLM和Llama等大型语言模型（LLMs）的快速发展显著改变了自然语言处理领域，展现出卓越的语言理解与生成能力。然而，一个根本性瓶颈依然存在：这些模型在处理需要复杂多步推理的任务时（尤其是数学问题求解）仍显不足。这一缺陷源于培养复杂推理能力所需的大规模、高质量、领域特定数据集的严重匮乏。为克服这一挑战，我们提出模板数据生成（TDG）——一种新颖且可扩展的范式，利用前沿LLM（GPT-4）自动生成参数化元模板，进而合成近乎无限的高质量问题与解决方案。基于该范式，我们创建了TemplateMath第一部分：TemplateGSM——一个包含超过700万个合成小学数学题的基础数据集。每个问题均配有可编程验证的解决方案，在规模上实现了前所未有的质量水平。该资源不仅解决了监督微调的数据稀缺问题，还通过可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）为模型对齐提供了稳健机制。我们的方法通过利用GPT-4生成元模板来增强数据扩充，确保问题结构的多样性与复杂性。通过提供数据与验证瓶颈的可扩展解决方案，TDG和TemplateGSM为新一代具备强大可靠推理能力的LLM铺平了道路。

They create TemplateMath Part I: TemplateGSM, a dataset of over 7 million grade school math problems with programmatically verifiable solutions, and demonstrate that this approach resolves data scarcity for supervised fine-tuning and enables model alignment via Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards, achieving unprecedented quality at scale.
该论文针对大型语言模型在复杂多步推理任务中因缺乏高质量领域特定数据集而表现不佳的瓶颈问题。作者提出了一种可扩展的模板化数据生成范式，利用GPT-4自动生成参数化元模板，进而合成大量高质量的问题与解答。他们构建了包含超过700万个小学算术问题的TemplateMath Part I: TemplateGSM数据集，每个问题都配有可编程验证的解答，实验表明该方法不仅解决了监督微调中的数据稀缺问题，还通过可验证奖励的强化学习实现了模型对齐，达到了前所未有的规模化质量水平。
WarmPrior: Straightening Flow-Matching Policies with Temporal Priors
Authors: Sinjae Kang, Chanyoung Kim, Kaixin Wang, Li Zhao, Kimin Lee
First: 2026-05-13T18:00:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T18:00:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative policies based on diffusion and flow matching have become a dominant paradigm for visuomotor robotic control. We show that replacing the standard Gaussian source distribution with WarmPrior, a simple temporally grounded prior constructed from readily available recent action history, consistently improves success rates on robotic manipulation tasks. We trace this gain to markedly straighter probability paths, echoing the effect of optimal-transport couplings in Rectified Flow. Beyond standard behavior cloning, WarmPrior also reshapes the exploration distribution in prior-space reinforcement learning, improving both sample efficiency and final performance. Collectively, these results identify the source distribution as an important and underexplored design axis in generative robot control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：WarmPrior：利用时间先验拉直流匹配策略
基于扩散和流匹配的生成策略已成为视觉运动机器人控制的主导范式。我们证明，用WarmPrior（一种从易于获取的近期动作历史构建的简单时间基础先验）替代标准高斯源分布，能持续提高机器人操作任务的成功率。我们将这一增益归因于显著更直的概率路径，这呼应了整流流中最优传输耦合的效果。除了标准行为克隆外，WarmPrior还重塑了先验空间强化学习中的探索分布，从而提高了样本效率和最终性能。总体而言，这些结果将源分布确定为生成式机器人控制中一个重要且未被充分探索的设计维度。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces WarmPrior, a method that replaces the standard Gaussian source distribution in diffusion and flow-matching generative policies for robotic control with a temporally grounded prior constructed from recent action history. This approach is motivated by the observation that the source distribution is an underexplored design axis, and it aims to straighten probability paths, similar to optimal-transport couplings in Rectified Flow. Experimental results on robotic manipulation tasks show that WarmPrior consistently improves success rates in behavior cloning and also enhances sample efficiency and final performance in prior-space reinforcement learning, demonstrating its effectiveness across different learning paradigms.
该论文提出了WarmPrior方法，将扩散和流匹配生成策略中标准的高斯源分布替换为基于近期动作历史构建的简单时间先验。其动机在于源分布是机器人控制生成策略中一个未被充分探索的设计维度，该方法旨在通过类似Rectified Flow中最优传输耦合的方式拉直概率路径。在机器人操作任务上的实验结果表明，WarmPrior在行为克隆中持续提升了成功率，并在先验空间强化学习中提高了样本效率和最终性能，验证了其在不同学习范式下的有效性。
BoostAPR: Boosting Automated Program Repair via Execution-Grounded Reinforcement Learning with Dual Reward Models
Authors: Yuanhao Li, Hongbo Wang, Xiaotang Shang, Xunzhu Tang, Yiming Cao, Xuhong Chen
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-05-09T19:31:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T16:38:24+00:00
Comments: 21 pages, 2 figures. Accepted at ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning for program repair is hindered by sparse execution feedback and coarse sequence-level rewards that obscure which edits actually fix bugs. We present BoostAPR, a three-stage framework addressing these challenges: (1) supervised fine-tuning on execution-verified demonstrations with reasoning traces, (2) training dual reward models--a sequence-level assessor and a line-level credit allocator--from execution outcomes, and (3) PPO optimization where the line-level model redistributes rewards to critical edit regions. This line-level credit assignment operates at an intermediate granularity naturally suited to code changes. Trained on SWE-Gym and evaluated on four benchmarks, BoostAPR achieves 40.7% on SWE-bench Verified (+22.9pp over base model), 24.8% on Defects4J (Python-to-Java transfer), 84.5% on HumanEval-Java, and 95.0% on QuixBugs, achieving competitive results among open-source models with strong cross-language generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BoostAPR：通过执行驱动的强化学习与双奖励模型提升自动程序修复
强化学习在程序修复中面临执行反馈稀疏和粗粒度序列级奖励掩盖实际修复编辑的挑战。我们提出BoostAPR，一个三阶段框架来解决这些问题：（1）在带有推理轨迹的执行验证演示上进行监督微调，（2）基于执行结果训练双奖励模型——序列级评估器和行级信用分配器，（3）PPO优化中行级模型将奖励重新分配到关键编辑区域。这种行级信用分配以自然适配代码变更的中间粒度运作。在SWE-Gym上训练并在四个基准上评估，BoostAPR在SWE-bench Verified上达到40.7%（比基础模型提升22.9个百分点），在Defects4J（Python到Java迁移）上达到24.8%，在HumanEval-Java上达到84.5%，在QuixBugs上达到95.0%，在开源模型中取得具有竞争力的结果，并展现出强大的跨语言泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
BoostAPR addresses the challenge of sparse execution feedback and coarse sequence-level rewards in reinforcement learning for automated program repair. The method introduces a three-stage framework: supervised fine-tuning on execution-verified demonstrations with reasoning traces, training dual reward models (a sequence-level assessor and a line-level credit allocator) from execution outcomes, and PPO optimization where the line-level model redistributes rewards to critical edit regions. Experimental results show that BoostAPR achieves 40.7% on SWE-bench Verified (a 22.9 percentage point improvement over the base model), 24.8% on Defects4J (demonstrating Python-to-Java transfer), 84.5% on HumanEval-Java, and 95.0% on QuixBugs, achieving competitive results among open-source models with strong cross-language generalization.
BoostAPR旨在解决强化学习在自动程序修复中因稀疏执行反馈和粗粒度序列级奖励而难以定位关键编辑的问题。该方法提出三阶段框架：首先在带有推理轨迹的执行验证演示上进行监督微调，然后从执行结果中训练双奖励模型（序列级评估器和行级信用分配器），最后通过PPO优化，由行级模型将奖励重新分配到关键编辑区域。实验结果表明，BoostAPR在SWE-bench Verified上达到40.7%（比基础模型提升22.9个百分点），在Defects4J上达到24.8%（展示Python到Java的跨语言迁移），在HumanEval-Java上达到84.5%，在QuixBugs上达到95.0%，在开源模型中取得具有竞争力的结果并展现出强大的跨语言泛化能力。
Rethinking Molecular OOD Generalization via Target-Aware Source Selection
Authors: Zhuohao Lin, Kun Li, Jiameng Chen, Jiajun Yu, Duanhua Cao, Yizhen Zheng, Wenbin Hu
First: 2026-05-13T16:09:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T16:09:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Robust prediction of molecular properties under extreme out-of-distribution (OOD) scenarios is a pivotal bottleneck in AI-driven drug discovery. Current scaffold-splitting protocols fail to obstruct microscopic semantic overlap, predisposing models to shortcut learning and overestimating their true extrapolation capability; meanwhile, conventional domain adaptation paradigms suffer under extreme structural shifts, as blindly aligning heterogeneous source libraries injects topological noise and triggers negative transfer. To address these two challenges, scaffold-cluster out-of-distribution performance evaluation benchmark (SCOPE-BENCH), a benchmark built on cluster-level partitioning in an explicit physicochemical descriptor space, is proposed alongside policy optimization for multi-source adaptation (POMA), a framework that formulates knowledge transfer as a retrieve-compose-adapt pipeline: labeled source scaffolds structurally close to the unlabeled target are first identified as proxy targets; a reinforcement learning policy then adaptively selects the optimal source subset from an exponentially large candidate pool; and dual-scale domain adaptation is finally performed at macroscopic topological and microscopic pharmacophore scales. Evaluations show that prediction errors of state-of-the-art 3D molecular models surge by up to 8.0x on SCOPE-BENCH with a mean of 5.9x, while POMA achieves up to an 11.2% reduction in mean absolute error with an average relative improvement of 6.2% across diverse backbone architectures. Code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Molecular-OOD-Code-73F6.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过目标感知源选择重新思考分子分布外泛化
在极端分布外场景下对分子性质进行稳健预测是AI驱动药物发现的关键瓶颈。当前的骨架划分协议无法阻止微观语义重叠，导致模型倾向于捷径学习并高估其真实外推能力；同时，传统域适应范式在极端结构偏移下表现不佳，因为盲目对齐异质源库会引入拓扑噪声并引发负迁移。为解决这两个挑战，本文提出了基于显式物理化学描述符空间簇级划分的基准SCOPE-BENCH，以及多源适应策略优化框架POMA，该框架将知识转移形式化为检索-组合-适应流程：首先识别与未标记目标结构接近的标记源骨架作为代理目标；然后通过强化学习策略从指数级候选池中自适应选择最优源子集；最后在宏观拓扑和微观药效团尺度上执行双尺度域适应。评估表明，最先进的3D分子模型在SCOPE-BENCH上的预测误差最高激增8.0倍（平均5.9倍），而POMA在不同骨干架构上平均绝对误差降低最高达11.2%，平均相对改进6.2%。代码见https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Molecular-OOD-Code-73F6。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses two key challenges in molecular out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization: current scaffold-splitting benchmarks allow microscopic semantic overlap, causing shortcut learning and overestimated extrapolation, while conventional domain adaptation fails under extreme structural shifts due to negative transfer from heterogeneous source libraries. To overcome these, the authors propose SCOPE-BENCH, a benchmark using cluster-level partitioning in physicochemical descriptor space, and POMA, a framework that formulates knowledge transfer as a retrieve-compose-adapt pipeline: it identifies source scaffolds structurally close to the unlabeled target as proxy targets, uses reinforcement learning to select the optimal source subset, and performs dual-scale domain adaptation at macroscopic topological and microscopic pharmacophore scales. Experimental results show that prediction errors of state-of-the-art 3D molecular models surge by up to 8.0x (mean 5.9x) on SCOPE-BENCH, while POMA achieves up to an 11.2% reduction in mean absolute error with an average relative improvement of 6.2% across diverse backbone architectures.
该论文针对分子分布外泛化中的两个关键挑战：当前骨架划分基准允许微观语义重叠，导致捷径学习和外推能力高估，而传统域适应在极端结构偏移下因异构源库的负迁移而失效。为此，作者提出了SCOPE-BENCH基准，基于理化描述符空间的簇级划分进行评估，以及POMA框架，将知识转移形式化为检索-组合-适应流程：先识别与无标签目标结构相近的有标签源骨架作为代理目标，再通过强化学习策略从指数级候选池中自适应选择最优源子集，最后在宏观拓扑和微观药效团尺度进行双尺度域适应。实验结果表明，在SCOPE-BENCH上，最先进的3D分子模型预测误差最高增加8.0倍（平均5.9倍），而POMA在不同骨干架构上实现了平均绝对误差最高降低11.2%，平均相对改进6.2%。
Tight Sample Complexity Bounds for Entropic Best Policy Identification
Authors: Amer Essakine, Claire Vernade
First: 2026-05-13T16:02:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T16:02:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study best-policy identification for finite-horizon risk-sensitive reinforcement learning under the entropic risk measure. Recent work established a constant gap in the exponential horizon dependence between lower and upper bounds on the number of samples required to identify an approximately optimal policy. Precisely, known lower bounds scale in $Ω(e^{|β| H})$ where $H$ is the horizon of the MDP, while the state-of-the-art upper bound achieves at best $O(e^{2|β| H})$ (arXiv:2506.00286v2) using a generative model. We show that this extra exponential factor can be traced to overly loose concentration control for exponential utilities. To close this open gap, we revisit the analysis of this problem through a forward-model based algorithm building on KL-based exploration bonuses that we adapt to the entropic criterion. The improvement we get is due to two main novel technical innovations. We leverage the smoothness properties of the exponential utility to derive sharper concentration bounds, and we propose a new stopping rule that exploits further this tightness to obtain a sample complexity that matches the lower bound.
中文标题/摘要
标题：熵风险最优策略识别的紧样本复杂度界
我们研究了熵风险度量下有限时域风险敏感强化学习的最优策略识别问题。近期工作揭示了在识别近似最优策略所需样本数量的下界与上界之间存在指数级时域依赖的常数差距。具体而言，已知下界以$Ω(e^{|β| H})$标度（其中$H$为MDP的时域长度），而当前最优上界在使用生成模型时仅能达到$O(e^{2|β| H})$（arXiv:2506.00286v2）。我们证明这一额外指数因子源于对指数效用函数过于宽松的集中性控制。为弥合这一开放差距，我们重新审视了该问题的分析，提出了一种基于前向模型的算法，该算法构建于针对熵准则调整的KL探索奖励之上。我们的改进源于两项主要技术创新：利用指数效用函数的平滑性推导更紧的集中性界，并提出一种新的停止规则以进一步利用这种紧性，从而获得与下界匹配的样本复杂度。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the sample complexity gap in best-policy identification for finite-horizon risk-sensitive reinforcement learning under the entropic risk measure. The motivation stems from a known discrepancy where lower bounds scale as Ω(e^{|β| H}) while existing upper bounds achieve only O(e^{2|β| H}), with H being the horizon. The authors propose a forward-model based algorithm that uses KL-based exploration bonuses adapted to the entropic criterion, incorporating two key innovations: sharper concentration bounds derived from the smoothness of exponential utilities, and a new stopping rule that exploits this tightness. The main experimental result is that the proposed method achieves a sample complexity matching the lower bound, thereby closing the open exponential gap.

Block-R1: Rethinking the Role of Block Size in Multi-domain Reinforcement Learning for Diffusion Large Language Models
Authors: Yan Jiang, Ruihong Qiu, Zi Huang
First: 2026-05-12T08:09:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T15:38:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recently, reinforcement learning (RL) has been widely applied during post-training for diffusion large language models (dLLMs) to enhance reasoning with block-wise semi-autoregressive generation. Block size has therefore become a vital factor in dLLMs, since it determines the parallel decoding granularity and affects the rollout trajectories during RL optimisation, e.g., GRPO. Instead of investigating the effect of block size during inference on individual domains, this paper studies block size from a domain conflict perspective for dLLM RL post-training in multi-domain scenarios. The main contributions are: (1) a formulation of domain block size conflict in multi-domain RL for dLLMs, which will largely affect the post-training effectiveness for rollout-based RL methods; (2) a novel dataset, Block-R1-41K is constructed with a best-improved training block size for each sample, which also induces a Block Size Conflict Score to quantitatively measure the domain conflict; (3) a new benchmark, Block-R1, for flexible RL post-training for dLLMs in both single and cross domain; and (4) a simple yet powerful cross-domain post-training method with sample-level best-improved training block sizes. Extensive experiments on 13 distinct datasets, 7 latest RL algorithms and diverse dLLM backbones are comprehensively covered in Block-R1. The benchmark is open-sourced at https://github.com/YanJiangJerry/Block-R1 with the dataset released at https://huggingface.co/datasets/YanJiangJerry/Block-R1-41K.

Decoupling Exploration and Policy Optimization: Uncertainty Guided Tree Search for Hard Exploration
Authors: Zakaria Mhammedi, James Cohan
First: 2026-03-23T17:56:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T15:33:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The process of discovery requires active exploration -- the act of collecting new and informative data. However, efficient autonomous exploration remains a major unsolved problem. The dominant paradigm addresses this challenge by using Reinforcement Learning (RL) to train agents with intrinsic motivation, maximizing a composite objective of extrinsic and intrinsic rewards. We suggest that this approach incurs unnecessary overhead: while policy optimization is necessary for precise task execution, employing such machinery solely to expand state coverage may be inefficient. In this paper, we propose a new approach that explicitly decouples exploration from policy optimization and bypasses RL entirely during the exploration phase. Our method uses a tree-search strategy inspired by the Go-With-The-Winner algorithm, paired with a measure of uncertainty to systematically drive exploration. By removing the overhead of policy optimization, our approach explores an order of magnitude more efficiently than standard intrinsic motivation baselines on hard exploration benchmarks. Further, we demonstrate that the trajectories discovered during exploration can be distilled into deployable policies using existing supervised backward learning algorithms, achieving state-of-the-art performance by a wide margin on Montezuma's Revenge, Pitfall!, and Venture without relying on domain-specific knowledge. Finally, we demonstrate the generality of our framework in high-dimensional continuous action spaces by solving the MuJoCo Adroit dexterous manipulation and AntMaze tasks in a sparse-reward setting, directly from image observations and without expert demonstrations or offline datasets. To the best of our knowledge, this has not been achieved before for the Adroit tasks.

标题：解耦探索与策略优化：面向困难探索任务的不确定性引导树搜索
发现过程需要主动探索——即收集新颖且信息丰富的数据。然而，高效自主探索仍是一个未解决的主要难题。主流范式通过强化学习训练具有内在动机的智能体，最大化外在奖励与内在奖励的复合目标来应对这一挑战。我们认为该方法存在不必要的开销：尽管策略优化对精确任务执行至关重要，但仅为了扩展状态覆盖而使用此类机制可能效率低下。本文提出一种新方法，将探索与策略优化明确解耦，并在探索阶段完全绕过强化学习。该方法采用受“赢家通吃”算法启发的树搜索策略，结合不确定性度量系统性地驱动探索。通过消除策略优化的开销，我们的方法在困难探索基准测试中的探索效率比标准内在动机基线高出一个数量级。此外，我们证明探索过程中发现的轨迹可通过现有监督反向学习算法蒸馏为可部署策略，在《蒙特祖玛的复仇》《陷阱！》和《冒险》等游戏中无需领域特定知识即大幅超越现有最优性能。最后，我们通过在高维连续动作空间中解决稀疏奖励设置的MuJoCo Adroit灵巧操控和AntMaze任务，直接基于图像观测且无需专家演示或离线数据集，展示了框架的通用性。据我们所知，这在Adroit任务中尚属首次实现。

Multi-Objective and Mixed-Reward Reinforcement Learning via Reward-Decorrelated Policy Optimization
Authors: Yang Bai, Kaiyuan Liu, Ziyuan Zhuang, Jiahong Zhou, Rongxiang Weng, Xin Chen, Jingang Wang, Xunliang Cai
First: 2026-05-13T15:05:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T15:05:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Complex reinforcement learning environments frequently employ multi-task and mixed-reward formulations. In these settings, heterogeneous reward distributions and correlated reward dimensions often destabilize the construction of scalar advantages. To address these challenges, we propose Reward-Decorrelated Policy Optimization (RDPO), a reward-processing method designed to explicitly target both failure modes. RDPO first utilizes Magnitude-Aware Quantile normalization to stabilize prompt-level advantage allocation across binary, fractional, and continuous rewards. It then applies Mahalanobis whitening within each active reward subspace to mitigate correlation redundancy prior to aggregation. When applied during the post-training of LongCat-Flash, RDPO enhances instruction following, writing quality, and robustness to hard prompts while remaining broadly competitive on reasoning and coding evaluations.
中文标题/摘要

Achieving $ε^{-2}$ Sample Complexity for Single-Loop Actor-Critic under Minimal Assumptions
Authors: Ishaq Hamza, Zaiwei Chen
First: 2026-05-13T15:04:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T15:04:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we establish last-iterate convergence rates for off-policy actor--critic methods in reinforcement learning. In particular, under a single-loop, single-timescale implementation and a broad class of policy updates, including approximate policy iteration and natural policy gradient methods, we prove the first $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ sample complexity guarantee for finding an $ε$-optimal policy under minimal assumptions, namely, the existence of a policy that induces an irreducible Markov chain. This stands in stark contrast to the existing literature, where an $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ sample complexity is achieved only through nested-loop updates and/or under strong, algorithm-dependent assumptions on the policies, such as uniform mixing and uniform exploration. Technically, to address the challenges posed by the coupled update equations arising from the single-loop implementation, as well as the potentially unbounded iterates induced by off-policy learning, our analysis is based on a coupled Lyapunov drift framework. Specifically, we establish a geometric convergence rate for the actor and an $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/T)$ convergence rate for the critic, and combine the two Lyapunov drift inequalities through a cross-domination property. We believe this analytical framework is of independent interest and may be applicable to other coupled iterative algorithms with unbounded
中文标题/摘要
标题：在最小假设下实现单循环演员-评论家的 $ε^{-2}$ 样本复杂度
本文建立了强化学习中离策略演员-评论家方法的最后迭代收敛速率。具体而言，在单循环、单时间尺度实现以及包括近似策略迭代和自然策略梯度方法在内的广泛策略更新类别下，我们证明了在最小假设（即存在一个能诱导不可约马尔可夫链的策略）下，找到 $ε$-最优策略的首个 $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ 样本复杂度保证。这与现有文献形成鲜明对比，现有文献中 $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ 样本复杂度仅通过嵌套循环更新和/或在强算法依赖假设（如均匀混合和均匀探索）下实现。技术上，为应对单循环实现带来的耦合更新方程以及离策略学习可能导致的无限迭代，我们的分析基于耦合李雅普诺夫漂移框架。具体而言，我们建立了演员的几何收敛速率和评论家的 $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/T)$ 收敛速率，并通过交叉支配性质结合两个李雅普诺夫漂移不等式。我们相信这一分析框架具有独立意义，并可能适用于其他具有无界迭代的耦合迭代算法。
